
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Express the family of unit segments with endpoints on the x- and y-axes in the first quadrant parametrically or algebraically.'}, {'objective': 'Determine the locus of points covered by these unit segments and characterize which points on segment AB are covered.'}, {'objective': 'Identify the unique point C on segment AB (excluding endpoints) that lies on no segment from the family other than AB itself.'}, {'objective': 'Calculate the squared distance OC^2 in simplest fraction form and find the sum of numerator and denominator.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- Points: O = (0,0), A = (1/2, 0), B = (0, √3/2).
- Segment AB connects A and B.
- Family \(\mathcal{F}\): all segments \(\overline{PQ}\) of length 1, with P on the x-axis (i.e., P = (x,0), x > 0) and Q on the y-axis (Q = (0,y), y > 0), lying in the first quadrant.
- There exists a unique point C on segment AB, distinct from A and B, such that C does not lie on any segment from \(\mathcal{F}\) except for \(\overline{AB}\) itself.
- Objective: Find \(OC^2 = \frac{p}{q}\) in lowest terms and compute \(p+q\).

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The segment AB lies between points A and B, which are on the positive x- and y-axes respectively.
- The family \(\mathcal{F}\) consists of all unit-length segments connecting a point on the x-axis to a point on the y-axis, both positive.
- The problem focuses on points on AB that are not covered by any segment in \(\mathcal{F}\) other than AB itself.
- The uniqueness of C implies a special geometric or metric property, likely related to the coverage of the first quadrant by these unit segments.
- The condition that C is distinct from A and B and lies on AB restricts the search to the interior of AB.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem is rooted in Euclidean geometry, specifically coordinate geometry.
- It involves geometric loci, segment lengths, and properties of points on line segments.
- The problem may also touch on optimization or uniqueness arguments within geometry.
- Such problems are common in mathematical competitions and advanced geometry contexts.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The exact nature of "does not belong to any segment from \(\mathcal{F}\) other than \(\overline{AB}\)" could be interpreted as C not lying on any other unit segment connecting the axes besides AB.
- The problem assumes the first quadrant, so P and Q are strictly positive on their respective axes.
- The uniqueness of C suggests a single exceptional point, but the reasoning or proof of uniqueness is not provided.
- It may be necessary to assume continuity and consider the parametric form of AB and the family \(\mathcal{F}\) to analyze coverage.
- Potential challenges include characterizing all segments in \(\mathcal{F}\) and determining which points on AB lie on these segments.

============== code generate 0 ================
async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Formally represent the family F of unit segments PQ with P=(x,0), Q=(0,y), x>0, y>0, and PQ=1. Express the condition x^2 + y^2 = 1 and parametrize these segments accordingly."
    cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1([taskInfo], cot_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, formalizing family F, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    subtask_desc1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking1, "answer": answer1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_instruction_2 = "Sub-task 2: Parametrize the segment AB with A=(1/2,0) and B=(0,sqrt(3)/2) using parameter t in [0,1], and express coordinates of any point C on AB as a function of t."
    cot_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_2,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agent_2([taskInfo], cot_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_2.id}, parametrizing AB, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")
    subtask_desc2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking2, "answer": answer2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc2)
    print("Step 2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_instruction_3 = "Sub-task 3: Formulate the condition for a point C on AB to lie on some segment PQ in F other than AB. Express C as a convex combination of P=(x,0) and Q=(0,y) with x>0, y>0, PQ=1."
    cot_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc3 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_3",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_3,
        "context": ["user query", thinking1, thinking2],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking3, answer3 = await cot_agent_3([taskInfo, thinking1, thinking2], cot_instruction_3, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_3.id}, formulating condition for C on AB to lie on other segments in F, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")
    subtask_desc3['response'] = {"thinking": thinking3, "answer": answer3}
    logs.append(subtask_desc3)
    print("Step 3: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_4 = "Sub-task 4: Analyze the uniqueness condition for the point C on AB that does not lie on any other segment from F except AB. Deduce necessary constraints and properties characterizing this unique point."
    N_sc = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_4 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0) for _ in range(N_sc)]
    possible_answers_4 = []
    possible_thinkings_4 = []
    subtask_desc4 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_4",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_4,
        "context": ["user query", thinking3],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N_sc):
        thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agents_4[i]([taskInfo, thinking3], cot_sc_instruction_4, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_4[i].id}, analyzing uniqueness condition, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
        possible_answers_4.append(answer4)
        possible_thinkings_4.append(thinking4)
    final_decision_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking4, answer4 = await final_decision_agent_4([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_4, "Sub-task 4: Synthesize and choose the most consistent answer for uniqueness condition." , is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")
    subtask_desc4['response'] = {"thinking": thinking4, "answer": answer4}
    logs.append(subtask_desc4)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_instruction_5 = "Sub-task 5: Combine parametric expressions and constraints from stage 0 to derive an explicit equation or system characterizing all points on AB that lie on some segment in F."
    cot_agent_5 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc5 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_5",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_5,
        "context": ["user query", thinking4],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }

    cot_agents_6 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0) for _ in range(N_sc)]
    possible_answers_6 = []
    possible_thinkings_6 = []
    subtask_desc6 = {

    }
    for i in range(N_sc):
        thinking6, answer6 = await cot_agents_6[i]([taskInfo, thinking5], cot_sc_instruction_6, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_6[i].id}, isolating parameter t for unique point C, thinking: {thinking6.content}; answer: {answer6.content}")
        possible_answers_6.append(answer6)
        possible_thinkings_6.append(thinking6)
    final_decision_agent_6 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking6, answer6 = await final_decision_agent_6([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_6, "Sub-task 6: Synthesize and choose the most consistent parameter t for unique point C." , is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 6 output: thinking - {thinking6.content}; answer - {answer6.content}")
    subtask_desc6['response'] = {"thinking": thinking6, "answer": answer6}
    logs.append(subtask_desc6)
    print("Step 6: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_instruction_7 = "Sub-task 7: Compute coordinates of unique point C on AB using parameter t from stage 1, and calculate OC^2 as fraction p/q in lowest terms."
    cot_agent_7 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc7 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_7",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_7,
        "context": ["user query", thinking6],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking7, answer7 = await cot_agent_7([taskInfo, thinking6], cot_instruction_7, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_7.id}, computing coordinates and OC^2, thinking: {thinking7.content}; answer: {answer7.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 7 output: thinking - {thinking7.content}; answer - {answer7.content}")
    subtask_desc7['response'] = {"thinking": thinking7, "answer": answer7}
    logs.append(subtask_desc7)
    print("Step 7: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    reflect_inst_8 = "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better."
    cot_reflect_instruction_8 = "Sub-task 8: Sum numerator p and denominator q of reduced fraction p/q for OC^2 to find final answer p+q." + reflect_inst_8
    cot_agent_8 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_8 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_8 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_8 = [taskInfo, thinking7]
    subtask_desc8 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_8",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_8,
        "context": ["user query", thinking7],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking8, answer8 = await cot_agent_8(cot_inputs_8, cot_reflect_instruction_8, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_8.id}, summing numerator and denominator, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_8):
        feedback8, correct8 = await critic_agent_8([taskInfo, thinking8], "Please review the answer above and criticize on where might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_8.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback8.content}; answer: {correct8.content}")
        if correct8.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_8.extend([thinking8, feedback8])
        thinking8, answer8 = await cot_agent_8(cot_inputs_8, cot_reflect_instruction_8, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_8.id}, refining sum calculation, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 8 output: thinking - {thinking8.content}; answer - {answer8.content}")
    subtask_desc8['response'] = {"thinking": thinking8, "answer": answer8}
    logs.append(subtask_desc8)
    print("Step 8: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking8, answer8, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

    thinking6, answer6 = await final_decision_agent_6([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_6, "Sub-task 6: Synthesize and output unique t in JSON format", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 6 output: thinking - {thinking6.content}; answer - {answer6.content}")
    subtask_desc6['response'] = {"thinking": thinking6, "answer": answer6}
    logs.append(subtask_desc6)
    print("Step 6: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_instruction_7 = (
        "Sub-task 7: Using parameter t from subtask 6, compute exact coordinates of C on AB, then calculate OC^2 symbolically. "
        "Simplify fully and extract numerator p and denominator q as explicit relatively prime positive integers. "
        "Return {\"p\": integer, \"q\": integer} in structured format."
    )
    cot_agent_7 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc7 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_7",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_7,
        "context": ["user query", thinking6.content, answer6.content, thinking2.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking7, answer7 = await cot_agent_7([taskInfo, thinking6, answer6, thinking2], cot_instruction_7, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_7.id}, computing p and q, thinking: {thinking7.content}; answer: {answer7.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 7 output: thinking - {thinking7.content}; answer - {answer7.content}")
    subtask_desc7['response'] = {"thinking": thinking7, "answer": answer7}
    logs.append(subtask_desc7)
    print("Step 7: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    reflect_inst_8 = (
        "Sub-task 8: Verify p and q from subtask 7 are relatively prime positive integers and that OC^2 = p/q satisfies rationality. "
        "Compute and output final answer p+q. Do not re-derive OC^2 or t; rely solely on verified values. Use Reflexion to cross-validate correctness and consistency before finalizing."
    )
    cot_reflect_instruction_8 = "Sub-task 8: Your problem is to verify and finalize the answer. " + reflect_inst_8
    cot_agent_8 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_8 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_8 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_8 = [taskInfo, thinking7, answer7]
    subtask_desc8 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_8",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_8,
        "context": ["user query", thinking7.content, answer7.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking8, answer8 = await cot_agent_8(cot_inputs_8, cot_reflect_instruction_8, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_8.id}, verifying final answer, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")
    for i in range(N_max_8):
        feedback8, correct8 = await critic_agent_8([taskInfo, thinking8], "Please review and provide limitations of the provided solution. If absolutely correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_8.id}, feedback: {feedback8.content}; correctness: {correct8.content}")
        if correct8.content.strip() == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_8.extend([thinking8, feedback8])
        thinking8, answer8 = await cot_agent_8(cot_inputs_8, cot_reflect_instruction_8, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_8.id}, refining answer, thinking: {thinking8.content}; answer: {answer8.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 8 output: thinking - {thinking8.content}; answer - {answer8.content}")
    subtask_desc8['response'] = {"thinking": thinking8, "answer": answer8}
    logs.append(subtask_desc8)
    print("Step 8: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking8, answer8, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Express the family of unit segments with endpoints on the x- and y-axes in the first quadrant parametrically or algebraically.'}, {'objective': 'Determine the locus of points covered by these unit segments and identify the unique point C on segment AB that lies outside this locus except on AB.'}, {'objective': 'Find the coordinates of point C on segment AB that satisfies the above condition.'}, {'objective': 'Calculate the squared distance OC^2 and simplify it to a fraction p/q in lowest terms, then compute p+q.'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- Points: O = (0,0), A = (1/2, 0), B = (0, sqrt(3)/2).
- Segment AB connects A and B.
- Family \(\mathcal{F}\): all segments \(\overline{PQ}\) of length 1 lying in the first quadrant, with P on the x-axis and Q on the y-axis.
- Objective: Identify the unique point C on segment AB (excluding endpoints A and B) such that C does not lie on any segment from \(\mathcal{F}\) other than \(\overline{AB}\) itself.
- Then compute \(OC^2 = \frac{p}{q}\) with p, q positive coprime integers, and find p + q.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The family \(\mathcal{F}\) consists of all unit-length segments with one endpoint on the x-axis and the other on the y-axis, both in the first quadrant.
- Each segment \(\overline{PQ}\) satisfies \(P = (x,0), Q = (0,y)\) with \(x,y > 0\) and \(x^2 + y^2 = 1\) (since length is 1).
- The union of all such segments forms a set of points connecting the axes with length 1.
- The segment AB lies inside the first quadrant, connecting A and B.
- The problem states there is a unique point C on AB (not A or B) that is not covered by any other segment in \(\mathcal{F}\) except AB itself.
- This implies that for all other segments in \(\mathcal{F}\), their union covers all points on AB except C.
- The uniqueness and exclusion condition suggests a geometric or measure-theoretic property of coverage by these segments.

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem is primarily in Euclidean geometry, specifically plane analytic geometry.
- It involves coordinate geometry, segment length constraints, and locus of points.
- Concepts of coverage and uniqueness relate to geometric measure or set theory aspects within geometry.
- Such problems are common in mathematical competitions and problem-solving contexts.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The exact nature of "does not belong to any segment from \(\mathcal{F}\) other than \(\overline{AB}\)" requires careful interpretation: does it mean C is not contained in the interior of any other segment in \(\mathcal{F}\)?
- The problem assumes the family \(\mathcal{F}\) includes all such segments of length 1 with endpoints on axes in the first quadrant, but the density or coverage of these segments on AB is not explicitly described.
- The uniqueness of C suggests a single exceptional point, but the reasoning behind this uniqueness is not given.
- Assumptions: The segments in \(\mathcal{F}\) are continuous and cover a region; the point C is interior to AB; the problem is well-posed with no degenerate cases.
- Potential challenge: characterizing the union of all such segments and identifying the unique uncovered point on AB.

We want to find the unique point C on AB such that C lies only on AB in F, i.e., no other segment PQ in F contains C. Equating C(t) = S(s) gives two equations: (1 - t)/2 = (1 - s)x and (t * sqrt(3))/2 = s y. From these, x = (1 - t)/(2(1 - s)) and y = (t * sqrt(3))/(2 s). Since x^2 + y^2 = 1, substituting x and y yields ((1 - t)^2)/(4(1 - s)^2) + (3 t^2)/(4 s^2) = 1. For a fixed t, this is an equation in s. The uniqueness condition means that the only solution s in (0,1) is s = t (corresponding to AB itself). To find such t, we analyze the equation for s and require that the equation has a unique solution s = t. Setting s = t in the equation, we get ((1 - t)^2)/(4(1 - t)^2) + (3 t^2)/(4 t^2) = 1/4 + 3/4 = 1, which is true. Improve instructions and context passing:\n   - Explicitly require agents to verify the rationality of OC² and provide detailed algebraic justifications.\n   - Include the envelope equation and problem constraints in the context for all relevant subtasks.\n\n7. Break down the final algebraic simplification into smaller, manageable subtasks if needed:\n   - Express OC² in terms of t.\n   - Substitute and simplify.\n   - Verify coprimality and positivity of p and q.\n\nBy embedding the envelope curve derivation and enforcing rigorous algebraic verification, the agents will avoid irrational dead ends and produce a correct, justified final answer consistent with the problem’s requirements.'}]

async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    # Stage 0: Formal representation and envelope derivation

    # Subtask 1: Represent family F of unit segments with endpoints on axes
    cot_instruction_0_1 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Formally represent the family F of unit-length segments \"\overline{PQ}\" "
        "with endpoints P=(x,0), Q=(0,y), where x,y>0 and x^2 + y^2 = 1. "
        "Express the parametric form of these segments and characterize the set of points covered by F as unions of such segments. "
        "Avoid solving for the unique point on AB at this stage; focus solely on formal representation and geometric interpretation.")
    cot_agent_0_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc_0_1 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_0.subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_0_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking_0_1, answer_0_1 = await cot_agent_0_1([taskInfo], cot_instruction_0_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_0_1.id}, representing family F, thinking: {thinking_0_1.content}; answer: {answer_0_1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking_0_1.content}; answer - {answer_0_1.content}")
    subtask_desc_0_1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_0_1, "answer": answer_0_1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_0_1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Subtask 2: Parametrize segment AB
    cot_instruction_0_2 = (
        "Sub-task 2: Parametrize the segment \"\overline{AB}\" with endpoints A=(1/2,0) and B=(0, sqrt(3)/2). "
        "Express any point C on \"\overline{AB}\" (excluding endpoints) as C(t) = ((1 - t)/2, (t * sqrt(3))/2) for t in (0,1). "
        "Avoid solving for t yet; focus on parametric form and geometric properties.")
    cot_agent_0_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc_0_2 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_0.subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_0_2,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking_0_2, answer_0_2 = await cot_agent_0_2([taskInfo], cot_instruction_0_2, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_0_2.id}, parametrizing segment AB, thinking: {thinking_0_2.content}; answer: {answer_0_2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking_0_2.content}; answer - {answer_0_2.content}")
    subtask_desc_0_2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_0_2, "answer": answer_0_2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_0_2)
    print("Step 2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Subtask 3: Derive envelope curve x^{2/3} + y^{2/3} = 1
    cot_instruction_0_3 = (
        "Sub-task 3: Derive rigorously the envelope curve of the family F of unit segments with endpoints on the axes in the first quadrant. "
        "Prove that the envelope satisfies the equation x^{2/3} + y^{2/3} = 1. "
        "Provide exact derivation and justification without numerical approximations.")
    cot_agent_0_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc_0_3 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_0.subtask_3",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_0_3,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_0_1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking_0_3, answer_0_3 = await cot_agent_0_3([taskInfo, thinking_0_1], cot_instruction_0_3, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_0_3.id}, deriving envelope curve, thinking: {thinking_0_3.content}; answer: {answer_0_3.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking_0_3.content}; answer - {answer_0_3.content}")
    subtask_desc_0_3['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_0_3, "answer": answer_0_3}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_0_3)
    print("Step 3: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Stage 1: Substitute C(t) into envelope and solve for t

    # Subtask 1: Substitute parametric C(t) into envelope equation
    cot_instruction_1_1 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Substitute the parametric form C(t) = ((1 - t)/2, (t * sqrt(3))/2) on segment AB into the envelope equation x^{2/3} + y^{2/3} = 1. "
        "Formulate the resulting algebraic equation in t exactly. Avoid numerical solving; provide precise algebraic form suitable for exact solution.")
    cot_agent_1_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc_1_1 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_1.subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_1_1,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_0_2.content, thinking_0_3.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking_1_1, answer_1_1 = await cot_agent_1_1([taskInfo, thinking_0_2, thinking_0_3], cot_instruction_1_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1_1.id}, substituting C(t) into envelope, thinking: {thinking_1_1.content}; answer: {answer_1_1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking_1_1.content}; answer - {answer_1_1.content}")
    subtask_desc_1_1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_1_1, "answer": answer_1_1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_1_1)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Subtask 2: Solve algebraic equation for unique t in (0,1) with SC_CoT
    cot_sc_instruction_1_2 = (
        "Sub-task 2: Based on the algebraic equation from Sub-task 1, solve exactly for the unique parameter t in (0,1) corresponding to point C on AB that lies on the envelope. "
        "Ensure the solution leads to a rational expression for OC^2. Avoid approximations or unjustified irrational expressions.")
    N = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_1_2 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0) for _ in range(N)]
    possible_answers_1_2 = []
    possible_thinkings_1_2 = []
    subtask_desc_1_2 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_1.subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_1_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_1_1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N):
        thinking_i, answer_i = await cot_agents_1_2[i]([taskInfo, thinking_1_1], cot_sc_instruction_1_2, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_1_2[i].id}, solving for t, thinking: {thinking_i.content}; answer: {answer_i.content}")
        possible_answers_1_2.append(answer_i)
        possible_thinkings_1_2.append(thinking_i)
    final_decision_agent_1_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking_1_2, answer_1_2 = await final_decision_agent_1_2([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_1_2, "Sub-task 2: Synthesize and choose the most consistent and correct solution for t.", is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking_1_2.content}; answer - {answer_1_2.content}")
    subtask_desc_1_2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_1_2, "answer": answer_1_2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_1_2)
    print("Step 5: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Stage 2: Compute OC^2 and sum p+q

    # Subtask 1: Compute OC^2 as reduced fraction p/q
    cot_instruction_2_1 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Compute OC^2 for the unique point C on AB found in Stage 1. Express OC^2 as a reduced fraction p/q with positive coprime integers p and q. "
        "Provide detailed algebraic simplification and verify rationality rigorously. Avoid irrational or approximate expressions.")
    cot_agent_2_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc_2_1 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_2.subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_2_1,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_1_2.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking_2_1, answer_2_1 = await cot_agent_2_1([taskInfo, thinking_1_2], cot_instruction_2_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_2_1.id}, computing OC^2 as fraction, thinking: {thinking_2_1.content}; answer: {answer_2_1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking_2_1.content}; answer - {answer_2_1.content}")
    subtask_desc_2_1['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_2_1, "answer": answer_2_1}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_2_1)
    print("Step 6: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    # Subtask 2: Calculate p + q from reduced fraction p/q with Reflexion
    reflect_inst_2_2 = (
        "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. "
        "Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better.")
    cot_reflect_instruction_2_2 = (
        "Sub-task 2: Calculate the sum p + q from the reduced fraction p/q obtained for OC^2. "
        "Use the simplified fraction from the previous subtask without re-deriving p and q. " + reflect_inst_2_2)
    cot_agent_2_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_2_2 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_2_2 = [taskInfo, thinking_2_1]
    subtask_desc_2_2 = {
        "subtask_id": "stage_2.subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_2_2,
        "context": ["user query", thinking_2_1.content],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking_2_2, answer_2_2 = await cot_agent_2_2(cot_inputs_2_2, cot_reflect_instruction_2_2, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_2_2.id}, calculating p+q, thinking: {thinking_2_2.content}; answer: {answer_2_2.content}")
    for i in range(N_max):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_2_2([taskInfo, thinking_2_2],
                                                  "Please review and provide the limitations of provided solutions. "
                                                  "If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'", i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_2_2.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_2_2.extend([thinking_2_2, feedback])
        thinking_2_2, answer_2_2 = await cot_agent_2_2(cot_inputs_2_2, cot_reflect_instruction_2_2, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_2_2.id}, refining p+q calculation, thinking: {thinking_2_2.content}; answer: {answer_2_2.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking_2_2.content}; answer - {answer_2_2.content}")
    subtask_desc_2_2['response'] = {"thinking": thinking_2_2, "answer": answer_2_2}
    logs.append(subtask_desc_2_2)
    print("Step 7: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking_2_2, answer_2_2, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs
